      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)" href="/user/show/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog">Suzanne (Under the Covers Book blog)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780141039510" href="/book/show/4638055-midnight-s-daughter">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=genre-urban-fantasy">genre-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=hero-mad-bad-and-dangerous-to-know">hero-mad-bad-and-dangerous-to-know</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=author-karen-chance">author-karen-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=va-va-voom-vampires">va-va-voom-vampires</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=paranormal-menagerie">paranormal-menagerie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=shifters">shifters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=mages-witches-magic-users">mages-witches-magic-users</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=heroines-i-love">heroines-i-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=faeries">faeries</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3575839-suzanne-under-the-covers-book-blog?shelf=action-adventure">action-adventure</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer102488273" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2752368071744597294">Dorina Basarab is a rare breed; dhampir, half human and half vampire. Hated by vampires but unable to fit in with humans she has carved her self out a niche; hunting rogue vampires, not something that endears her to the vamp. But, when her father come calling needing her help with a family matter, her ruthless and insane uncle <i>the</i> Dracula has escaped from his prison and is once again on the loose and gunning for all those who helped imprison him, with Dory at the top of the list...<br/><br/>What a fantast</span>
  <span id="freeText2752368071744597294" style="display:none">Dorina Basarab is a rare breed; dhampir, half human and half vampire. Hated by vampires but unable to fit in with humans she has carved her self out a niche; hunting rogue vampires, not something that endears her to the vamp. But, when her father come calling needing her help with a family matter, her ruthless and insane uncle <i>the</i> Dracula has escaped from his prison and is once again on the loose and gunning for all those who helped imprison him, with Dory at the top of the list...<br /><br />What a fantastic read! Karen Chance has started off her new series, an offshoot of her <i>Cassie Palmer</i> series, with a bang. This is a fast paced, action packed and enthralling read. <br /><br />If you have read the <i>Cassie Palmer</i> series then some of the characters will be very familiar to you and I love how all the people across both the series tie up. Dory is Mircea's daughter, one of the main characters from the <i>Cassie Palmer</i> series, and although he is no doubt a fearsome vampire, a fantastic diplomat and a fabulous lover, his dad skills require a little work. Raised as an outcast and relying only on herself Dory is one of the tough-as-nails, kick ass heroines who isn't afraid to rush head first into fight, most of the time without thinking through the consequences. I adored her! <br /><br />As this was a first book there was quite alot of information thrown at you, but as I had read the <i>Cassie Palmer</i> series most it was familiar. But the world that Karen Chance has crafterd over these two series is interesting and very well thought out. <br /><br />There was also a little romance and alot of sexual tension between Dory and Louis-Cesare (another familiar face!) that vampire that Dory has been forced to work with to help bring down Dracula. It was contempy on first sight for both of them, but I loved seeing their opnion change as they got to know eachother properly and I can't wait to see what happens next between them in <i>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6203049.Death_s_Mistress__Dorina_Basarab___2_" title="Death's Mistress (Dorina Basarab, #2) by Karen Chance" rel="nofollow noopener">Death's Mistress</a>
</i> the next book. <br /><br /><i>Midnight's Daughter</i> had fast paced action, magic and a little bit of romance all the best ingredients to make an unputdownable read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="2752368071744597294" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_139190956" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/139190956" />
    <a title="Isa Lavinia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1016831-isa-lavinia"><img alt="Isa Lavinia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1518528816p2/1016831.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/139190956?book_show_action=true">Jan 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Isa Lavinia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Isa Lavinia" href="/user/show/1016831-isa-lavinia">Isa Lavinia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=worth-re-reading">worth-re-reading</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=favourites">favourites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=love-hate">love-hate</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1016831-isa-lavinia?shelf=series-i-follow">series-i-follow</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer139190956" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10479291676734669754"><a href='http://paperbackwonderland.blogspot.pt/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380238999i/681674.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/><b>actual rating 4.5 stars</b><br/><br/>I absolutely LOVE this series - at the moment, this and <i>Downside Ghosts</i> are the only Urban Fantasy series that haven't disappointed me <i>
  <s>*cough cough* Kate Daniels *cough cough*</s>
</i>. And, as usual, when I love something, I keep postponing my reviews because distance helps me get out of the ~<i>omg fangirl!!!</i>~ mindset and see the series strengths more clearly.<br/><br/>Karen Chance introduces us to the peculiar life of Dorina Basarab, a Dhampir - daughter of the vampire Senator Mirce</span>
  <span id="freeText10479291676734669754" style="display:none"><a href="http://paperbackwonderland.blogspot.pt/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380238999i/681674.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br><b>actual rating 4.5 stars</b><br><br>I absolutely LOVE this series - at the moment, this and <i>Downside Ghosts</i> are the only Urban Fantasy series that haven't disappointed me <i>
  <s>*cough cough* Kate Daniels *cough cough*</s>
</i>. And, as usual, when I love something, I keep postponing my reviews because distance helps me get out of the ~<i>omg fangirl!!!</i>~ mindset and see the series strengths more clearly.<br><br>Karen Chance introduces us to the peculiar life of Dorina Basarab, a Dhampir - daughter of the vampire Senator Mircea Basarab (of the <i>Cassie Palmer</i> series, which I haven't really read and, quite frankly, don't think they're my cup of tea).<br><br>Dorina's best friend and roommate, Claire, has a gift: her presence dampens others' magical abilities. Seeing as Dorina, as a dhampir, is prone to blackouts during which she experiences uncontrollable rages and awakes surrounded by carnage (reason as to why most dhampirs lead very short lives), Claire is a very handy friend to have, even if it weren't for the genuine friendship between her and Dory. <br><br>...That is, until Claire goes missing and word on the street is that she was taken by a vampire - evidence leads to Dory's uncle Dracula.<br><br>Dorina's father, Mircea, wants Dorina to recapture Dracula, and for that mission she has to team up with the Master Vampire Louis-Cesare, the only vampire Dorina's eccentric uncle Radu Basarab "made". <br>But the mission doesn't turn out to be as straightforward as they thought...<br><br>What has me absolutely obsessed with this series is Dorina's relationship with her father, Mircea. <br>Dorina's memories are fractured. She longs for her father's love and approval, and he, in turn, seems to yearn to bestow upon her all the tenderness of a loving father... but, as with most well written relationships, things are extremely complicated between them.<br><br>If you're looking for a well researched series, featuring POC in positions of power, LGBT characters with vital roles in the plot, fast paced action, a complete lack of sappiness, a hot dash of romance, and hilarious situations, then this is the series for <u>
  <b>you</b>
</u>!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10479291676734669754" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_537588159" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/537588159" />
    <a title="Marsha" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1991207-marsha"><img alt="Marsha" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1277752983p2/1991207.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/537588159?book_show_action=true">Feb 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marsha" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marsha" href="/user/show/1991207-marsha">Marsha</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Adult Urban Fantasy Lovers</span></div>

        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer537588159" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13604557144918316868">"Midnight's Daughter" is the second book I've read by Karen Chance and my opinion of her storytelling skills has not changed. I did not enjoy the first book I read by her and did not enjoy this book as well.<br/><br/>Dorina is a dhampir, half vampire ans half human. As a half breed she is looked down upon by most supernatural. When her roommate, Claire goes missing for a month, Dorina is rechecking her leads for the remotest of clues. Tgen, her father calls her in to ask for assistance in recapturing her </span>
  <span id="freeText13604557144918316868" style="display:none">"Midnight's Daughter" is the second book I've read by Karen Chance and my opinion of her storytelling skills has not changed. I did not enjoy the first book I read by her and did not enjoy this book as well.<br /><br />Dorina is a dhampir, half vampire ans half human. As a half breed she is looked down upon by most supernatural. When her roommate, Claire goes missing for a month, Dorina is rechecking her leads for the remotest of clues. Tgen, her father calls her in to ask for assistance in recapturing her uncle, the dreaded, Dracula. Her father promises to locate Claire if Dorina duplicate Dracula.<br /><br />To assist her in this cause, Daddy dearest saddles Dorina with Louis Cesare, a stuck up vampire who makes his dislike of Dorina known from the start. If they are to locate Dracula they will need to work together. Soon rumors emerge indicating that Claire may be pregnant by the Prince of fae, making her child a direct heir to the throne and causing the fae to get involved in the search as well.<br /><br />Before Dorina can confirm the rumors she stumbles upon an illegal auction of horrible, genetically altered creatures that leaves her sick to her stomach. As she takes down the auction, she is left with one stinky creature who believes she is it's savior.<br /><br />With a plot like this, normally I would be all over it. So, what is my problem with this book? First and foremost, Ms Chance likes to write out long drawn out explanations, dreams, character thoughts but does not balance it out with sufficient dialogue. You can read 9-12 pages of ramblings before getting to two or three paragraphs of dialogue.<br /><br />I cannot believe I am going to say this but this book also had too much action! Normally I enjoyed good action scenes but in this book it was overkill to the point I found myself weary. Another issue for me is that I hate it when author write phrases in a foreign language and then don't use sufficient context clues to help the reader translate. Ugh!<br /><br />All and all, I have come to the conclusion that I am just not a fan of the writing of Karen Chance and probably never will be. I know she has a great following and that is great. Different strokes for different folks. Read it for yourself and decide. Needless to say I will not be going on to read any more books in this series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13604557144918316868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('+tVmmrOZzh28rTwMJA9syDAOc92dNL50kp0ihKScL/LaM8M7i1IX69HId8VyQVoOq/5t105c9ib7JKF8E4Lppw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('L3I6PzQMxwvSDbs2Z4Q0g7roxRXtyY9qkH9RUZq7unwPlJ+eDMce/b9o8P8xygJFIRjbHz6hxzj5xtKpLaV8KQ==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText9461315054255595139" style="display:none">Karen Chance is the author of two New York Times bestselling series, plus a number of novellas and short stories, all set in the Cassandra Palmer universe. A full-time writer since 2008, she was previously a university history teacher, which comes in handy when writing the time-travel aspect of Cassie’s crazy adventures.             var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
